    </span></span></div></div></div><p class="markdown-p"><span>A record that includes all details of a transaction, including current </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#status"><span>status</span></a><span>.</span></p><div><div><h5>Server-side response object returned directly or within a successful<!-- --> ariel-label="acquirer_reference_number">acquirer_reference_number</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>A unique number that tags a credit or debit card transaction when it goes from the merchants bank through to the cardholder&#x27;s bank. </p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="bin"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#bin" ariel-label="bin">bin</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The first 6 digits of the card number, also known as the Bank Identification Number (BIN). Also includes an identifier for the account (e.g. last 4 digits if the payment method was a credit card).</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="token"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#token" ariel-label="token">token</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>An alphanumeric value that references a specific payment method stored in your Vault. Value will be <code>nil</code> if the transaction was not created from a vaulted Apple Pay card.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="authorization_adjustments"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#authorization_adjustments" ariel-label="authorization_adjustments">authorization_adjustments</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>A collection of <a href="#authorization-adjustments">authorization adjustments</a> associated with the transaction.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="authorization_expires_at"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#authorization_expires_at" ariel-label="authorization_expires_at">authorization_expires_at</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">Time</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">The date/time the transaction will expire if it has the <span class="formatConstant">authorized</span> status. For more details on authorization expiration timeframes, see the <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#authorization-expired">Statuses reference</a>. Returned in UTC.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="avs_error_response_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#avs_error_response_code" ariel-label="avs_error_response_code">avs_error_response_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">This field is populated if there was an error when checking AVS or the processing bank does not support AVS. Possible values:</p>
<ul class=" list list--disc">
<li><code>S</code> = Issuing bank does not support AVS</li>
<li><code>E</code> = AVS system error</li>
</ul>
<br/>
<p class=" markdown-p">If this value is <!-- -->nil<!-- -->, you will see responses in both <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby#avs_postal_code_response_code">avs_postal_code_response_code</a></code> and <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby#avs_street_address_response_code">avs_street_address_response_code</a></code>.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="avs_postal_code_response_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#avs_postal_code_response_code" ariel-label="avs_postal_code_response_code">avs_postal_code_response_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>This is populated if the processor supports the address verification system (AVS). Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>M</code> = Matches</li><li><code>N</code> = Does not match</li><li><code>U</code> = Not verified</li><li><code>I</code> = Not provided</li><li><code>A</code> = Not applicable</li><li><code>B</code> = Bypass</li></ul></div></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="avs_street_address_response_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#avs_street_address_response_code" ariel-label="avs_street_address_response_code">avs_street_address_response_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>This is populated if the processor supports the address verification system (AVS). Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>M</code> = Matches</li><li><code>N</code> = Does not match</li><li><code>U</code> = Not verified</li><li><code>I</code> = Not provided</li><li><code>A</code> = Not applicable</li><li><code>B</code> = Bypass</li></ul></div></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="billing_details"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#billing_details" ariel-label="billing_details">billing_details</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">map</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The billing address details used to process this transaction. If billing address was stored in the Vault, then the billing address details are a snapshot of the address in the Vault at the time the transaction was created. </span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="company"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#company" ariel-label="company">company</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The billing company name. See the <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale">transaction API requests section</a> for details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="country_code_alpha2"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#country_code_alpha2" ariel-label="country_code_alpha2">country_code_alpha2</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The 2-letter billing <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/countries">country code</a>. See the <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale">transaction API requests section</a> for details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="country_code_alpha3"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#country_code_alpha3" ariel-label="country_code_alpha3">country_code_alpha3</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The 3-letter billing <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/countries">country code</a>. See the <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale">transaction API requests section</a> for details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="country_code_numeric"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#country_code_numeric" ariel-label="country_code_numeric">country_code_numeric</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The numeric billing <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/countries">country code</a>. See the <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale">transaction API requests section</a> for details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="country_name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#country_name" ariel-label="country_name">country_name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The billing country name. See the <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale">transaction API requests section</a> for details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="extended_address"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#extended_address" ariel-label="extended_address">extended_address</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The extended billing address. See the <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale">transaction API requests section</a> for details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#id" ariel-label="id">id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The billing details ID. A customer Vault record can contain up to 50 shipping and billing addresses, each with a unique ID. See the <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale">transaction API requests section</a> for details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="international_phone"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#international_phone" ariel-label="international_phone">international_phone</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">map</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The phone number that belongs to the address that is structured with country code and national number.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-2 type-string api-table-row " id="country_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#country_code" ariel-label="country_code">country_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Country code of phone number. 1-3 digits. Required.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-2 type-string api-table-row " id="national_number"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#national_number" ariel-label="national_number">national_number</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>National number of phone number. 4-12 digits. Required.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="last_name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#last_name" ariel-label="last_name">last_name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The last name. For PayPal transactions, this maps to the PayPal account&#x27;s <code>bn_code</code>.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="created_at"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#created_at" ariel-label="created_at">created_at</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">Time</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The date/time the object was created. Returned in UTC.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="credit_card_details"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#credit_card_details" ariel-label="credit_card_details">credit_card_details</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">map</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">If <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby#payment_instrument_type">payment_instrument_type</a></code> is <span class="langAttribute">credit_card</span>, these are the details of the card used for the transaction. If the transaction was created using Vault tokens, then this attribute is a snapshot of the credit card in the Vault at the time the transaction was created.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="bin"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#bin" ariel-label="bin">bin</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The first 6 digits of the credit card, known as the bank identification number (BIN).</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="business"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#business" ariel-label="business">business</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">enum</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">Whether the card is a business card. </p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="expiration_date"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#expiration_date" ariel-label="expiration_date">expiration_date</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The expiration date, formatted <code>MM/YY</code> or <code>MM/YYYY</code>. May be used instead of expiration month and expiration year.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="expiration_month"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#expiration_month" ariel-label="expiration_month">expiration_month</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The expiration month of the credit card used, formatted <code>MM</code>.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="expiration_year"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#expiration_year" ariel-label="expiration_year">expiration_year</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The expiration year of the credit card used, formatted <code>YYYY</code>.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="healthcare"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#healthcare" ariel-label="healthcare">healthcare</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">enum</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">Whether the card is a healthcare card. <ul class=" list list--disc">
<li><code>Braintree::CreditCard::HealthCare::Yes</code></li>
<li><code>Braintree::CreditCard::HealthCare::No</code></li>
<li><code>Braintree::CreditCard::HealthCare::Unknown</code></li>
</ul>

</p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="token"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#token" ariel-label="token">token</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">The Vault token for the credit card. Unlike other attributes in this details map, this attribute is not a snapshot  if you update the payment method token after creating a transaction, the <span class="langAttribute">credit_card_details.token</span> attribute will return the new value rather than the value associated with the transaction at the time it was created. See the <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale">transaction API requests section</a> for additional details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="unique_number_identifier"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#unique_number_identifier" ariel-label="unique_number_identifier">unique_number_identifier</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>A randomly-generated string that uniquely identifies a credit card number in the Vault. If the same credit card is added to a merchant&#x27;s Vault multiple times, each Vault entry will have the same unique identifier. This value is randomly generated by merchant gateway account, so it will be different for each merchant&#x27;s Vault.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="currency_iso_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#currency_iso_code" ariel-label="currency_iso_code">currency_iso_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The currency for the transaction (e.g. &quot;USD&quot; for US dollars). <li><code>Braintree::CreditCard::CustomerLocation::US</code></li>

<li><code>Braintree::CreditCard::CustomerLocation::US</code></li>

See the <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/guides/ach/overview">ACH Direct Debit guide</a> for details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="account_holder_name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#account_holder_name" ariel-label="account_holder_name">account_holder_name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Account holder name.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="account_type"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#account_type" ariel-label="account_type">account_type</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>The type of the bank account. <p class=" markdown-p"><strong>Venmo payments are currently in a limited release and are only available to select merchants</strong>. See the <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/guides/venmo/overview">Venmo guide</a> for details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="image_url"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#image_url" ariel-label="image_url">image_url</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>A URL that points to a payment method image resource (a PNG file) hosted by Braintree.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="source_description"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#source_description" ariel-label="source_description">source_description</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>A short description of the payment method, including the Venmo username.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="token"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#token" ariel-label="token">token</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>An alphanumeric value that references a specific payment method stored in your Vault. Unlike other attributes in this details map, this attribute is not a snapshot  if you update the payment method token after creating a transaction, the <span class="langAttribute">visa_checkout_card_details.token</span> attribute will return the new value rather than the value associated with the transaction at the time it was created. See the <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale">transaction API requests section</a> for additional details.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="voice_referral_number"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#voice_referral_number" ariel-label="voice_referral_number">voice_referral_number</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The value passed by the merchant with a <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses">voice-authorized transaction</a>.</p></p></span></div></div></div></div><h2 id="result-object" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Result object</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#result-object" aria-label="Result object"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>Read more about </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/result-objects/ruby"><span>result objects</span></a><span>.</span></p><h3 id="successful-result" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Successful result</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#successful-result" aria-label="Successful result"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><div><span>If the result is successful, the transaction will have either a
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#settling"><span>settling status</span></a><span>,
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#authorized"><span>authorized status</span></a><span>, or (if the </span><code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#options-submit_for_settlement">options-submit_for_settlement</a></code><span> option was used) a </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#submitted-for-settlement"><span>submitted for settlement status</span></a><span>.
</span></div><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.success?
#=&gt; true

transaction = result.transaction
transaction.status
#=&gt; &quot;authorized&quot;</code></pre></div></div></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Additionally, you may inspect the result to determine if the transaction was created using a
    specific payment method type (e.g. PayPal account or a credit card), using the provided format.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">transaction = result.transaction
transaction.payment_instrument_type == PaymentInstrumentType::PayPalAccount
#=&gt; false
transaction.payment_instrument_type == PaymentInstrumentType::CreditCard
#=&gt; true</code></pre></div></div></p><h3 id="unsuccessful-result" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Unsuccessful result</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#unsuccessful-result" aria-label="Unsuccessful result"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><div><span>Success will return </span><span class="langAttribute">{false}</span><span> if:</span></div><ul class="list list--disc"><li><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#validation-errors"><span>Validations</span></a><span> prevent the transaction from being created</span></li><li><span>The processor </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#processor-declined"><span>declines the authorization</span></a><span> or
        </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#processor-settlement-declined"><span>settlement</span></a></li><li><span>The </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#gateway-rejection"><span>gateway rejects</span></a><span> the transaction</span></li></ul><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.success?
#=&gt; false

result.errors</code></pre></div></div></p><h4 id="validation-errors" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Validation errors</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#validation-errors" aria-label="Validation errors"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><div><span>If any parameters are invalid, then the success call will return </span><code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><span class="langAttribute">{false}</span></code><span> and the </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/result-objects"><span>result object</span></a><span>
    will contain one or more </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/validation-errors/all"><span>validation errors</span></a><span>
    indicating which parameters were invalid.</span></div><div><span>When receiving a validation error, a </span><code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><formatresponseobject value="transaction"></formatresponseobject></code><span> object will not be
    present on the </span><code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><formatvariable value="result"></formatvariable></code><span> object.</span></div><h4 id="processor-declined" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Processor declined</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#processor-declined" aria-label="Processor declined"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><p class="markdown-p"><span>If the processor
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#processor-declined"><span>declines the transaction during the authorization</span></a><span>,
    the
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses"><span>processor response</span></a><span>
    will be available on the transaction object.
</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.success?
#=&gt; false
result.transaction.status
#=&gt; &quot;processor_declined&quot;

result.transaction.processor_response_type
#=&gt; &quot;soft_declined&quot;
result.transaction.processor_response_code
#=&gt; &quot;2001&quot;
result.transaction.processor_response_text
#=&gt; &quot;Insufficient Funds&quot;</code></pre></div></div></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>As a supplement to the standardized processor response codes, we will return bank-specific
    Additional Processor Responses on the transaction object. The standardized code is what you should
    use when handling the result object, but the Additional Processor Response might provide further
    context.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.transaction.additional_processor_response
# e.g. &quot;05 : NOT AUTHORISED&quot;</code></pre></div></div></p><h4 id="processor-settlement-declined" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Processor settlement declined</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#processor-settlement-declined" aria-label="Processor settlement declined"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><p class="markdown-p"><span>If the processor
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#settlement-declined"><span>declines the transaction at the settlement stage</span></a><span>,
    the </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/settlement-responses"><span>processor response</span></a><span>
    will be available on the transaction object.
</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.success?

#=&gt; &quot;Settlement Declined&quot;</code></pre></div></div></p><h4 id="gateway-rejection" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Gateway rejection</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#gateway-rejection" aria-label="Gateway rejection"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><p class="markdown-p"><span>If the transaction is
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#gateway-rejected"><span>rejected by the gateway</span></a><span> based on your
    account settings, you can check for the transaction status and gateway rejection reason.
</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.success?
#=&gt; false
result.transaction.status
#=&gt; &quot;gateway_rejected&quot;
result.transaction.gateway_rejection_reason
#=&gt; e.g. &quot;cvv&quot;</code></pre></div></div></p><h4 id="risk-data" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Risk data</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#risk-data" aria-label="Risk data"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><p class="markdown-p"><span>We return the risk data on credit card verifications and on transactions with
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/guides/premium-fraud-management-tools/overview#compatibility"><span>all compatible payment methods</span></a><span>.
    The data includes the fraud service provider, the risk identifier, the device data captured flag,
    and the risk decision, which can provide further context on how a verification or transaction was
    scored by our Premium Fraud Management Tools. For users of Fraud Protection, the data will include
    the decision reasons. For users of Fraud Protection Advanced, the data will also include the risk
    score.
</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><style data-emotion="css 4757ty-svg-size_xs">.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs{speak:none;display:inline-block;aspect-ratio:1;width:1.125rem;height:1.125rem;}.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs img,.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs svg{width:100%;height:100%;display:block;}</style><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__title__FOcbD">Note</span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"></span></div></div></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>{' '}
            For users of our Java and .NET SDKs, you will need to upgrade to versions .NET 5.4.0 and Java 3.7.0
            or later to see the decision reasons and risk score in the risk data.{' '}</span></p><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.transaction.risk_data.id
#=&gt; &quot;1SG23YHM4BT5&quot;
result.transaction.risk_data.decision
#=&gt; &quot;Decline&quot;
result.transaction.risk_data.device_data_captured
#=&gt; true
result.transaction.risk_data.fraud_service_provider
#=&gt; &quot;Kount&quot;
result.transaction.risk_data.decision_reasons
#=&gt; [&quot;reason1&quot;, &quot;reason2&quot;]
result.transaction.risk_data.risk_score
#=&gt; 42</code></pre></div></div><p class="markdown-p"></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>The possible values of the risk decision are:</span></p><ul class="list list--disc"><li><span>"Not Evaluated"</span></li><li><span>"Approve"</span></li><li><span>"Review"</span></li><li><span>"Decline"</span></li></ul><h4 id="params-retrieval" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Params retrieval</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#params-retrieval" aria-label="Params retrieval"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><p class="markdown-p"><span>See our documentation on </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/result-objects/ruby#params"><span>result objects</span></a><span>.</span></p><h2 id="examples" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Examples</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#examples" aria-label="Examples"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><h3 id="currencies" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Currencies</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#currencies" aria-label="Currencies"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><p class="markdown-p"><span>Each merchant account can only process transactions for a single currency.
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#specify-merchant-account-id"><span>Setting which merchant account to use</span></a><span> will also determine which currency the transaction is processed with.
</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.transaction.currency_iso_code
#=&gt; &quot;USD&quot;</code></pre></div></div></p><h3 id="settlement-status" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Settlement status</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#settlement-status" aria-label="Settlement status"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><div><span>Check the result for success, and if it has failed, then first check for validation errors. If there
    are no validation errors, inspect the </span><code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><span class="langAttribute">processor_settlement_response_code</span></code><span>
    on the transaction, which will indicate if the processor declined the request.</span></div><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">if result.success?
  # transaction successfully submitted for settlement
elsif result.errors.any?
  puts result.errors.inspect
else
  puts result.transaction.processor_settlement_response_code
  puts result.transaction.processor_settlement_response_text
end</code></pre></div></div></p><h4 id="processor-settlement-declined" class="test_h4 markdown-h4"><span>Processor settlement declined</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#processor-settlement-declined" aria-label="Processor settlement declined"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h4><p class="markdown-p"><span>If the settlement request is declined by the processor, the
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/settlement-responses"><span>processor response</span></a><span>
    will be available on the transaction object.
</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">result.success?
#=&gt; false
result.transaction.status
#=&gt; &quot;settlement_declined&quot;
result.transaction.processor_settlement_response_code
#=&gt; &quot;4001&quot;
result.transaction.processor_settlement_response_text
#=&gt; &quot;Settlement Declined&quot;</code></pre></div></div></p><h3 id="voiding-settlement" class="test_h3 markdown-h3"><span>Voiding settlement</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#voiding-settlement" aria-label="Voiding settlement"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h3><p class="markdown-p"><span>If you submit a transaction for settlement and then decide you actually don't want to settle it, you
    can </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/void"><span>void</span></a><span> it before it's settled. After it's
    settled, you'll need to </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/refund"><span>refund</span></a><span> it instead.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>To check if the transaction has been settled, find the transaction and check the status.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">transaction = gateway.transaction.find(&quot;the_transaction_id&quot;)
    if transaction.status == &quot;submitted_for_settlement&quot;
      # can void
    elsif transaction.status == &quot;settled&quot;
      # will have to refund it
    else
      # this example only expected one of the two above statuses
    end</code></pre></div></div></p><h2 id="authorization-adjustments" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Authorization adjustments</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#authorization-adjustments" aria-label="Authorization adjustments"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>The authorized amount of a transaction can be adjusted by using the
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/adjust-authorization"><span>adjust authorization</span></a><span> endpoint.
    This will cause an authorization adjustment to be performed.
</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>When submitting a transaction for settlement, if you
    </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/submit-for-settlement/ruby#specifying-settlement-amount"><span>specify a settlement amount that is different than the authorized amount</span></a><span>,
    an authorization adjustment may be performed automatically.
</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>For each adjustment performed, an authorization adjustment object will be associated with the
    original transaction. These adjustment objects will include the following details:</span></p><style data-emotion="css class="langAttribute">amount</span></td><td><span>
                The difference between the authorized amount and the amount submitted for settlement.
                Negative values indicate the authorized amount was adjusted down.
            </span></td></tr><tr id="adjustment-detail-success" class="selectable-row"><td><span class="langAttribute">success</span></td><td><span>A boolean value indicating if the adjustment was successful.</span></td></tr><tr id="adjustment-detail-timestamp" class="selectable-row"><td><span class="langAttribute">timestamp</span></td><td><span>The date/time when the adjustment was performed.</span></td></tr><tr id="adjustment-detail-proccessorresponsetype" class="selectable-row"><td><span class="langAttribute">proccessor_response_type</span></td><td><span>

                The processor response text. See the list of{' '}
                </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses" pa-marked="1"><span>
                    possible processor authorization responses.
                </span></a></td></tr></tbody></table><h2 id="status-history-details" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Status history details</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link"                 Status Detail
                </span><p class="markdown-p"></p></th><th><span>Description</span></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><span class="langAttribute">amount</span></td><td><span>The amount of the request.</span></td></tr><tr><td><span class="langAttribute">status</span></td><td><span>
                A record of the statuses that a transaction has progressed through.
                Possible values:
                </span><ul class="list list--disc list list--disc"><li><span class="langAttribute">authorization_expired</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">authorized</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">authorizing</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">settlement_pending</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">settlement_confirmed</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">settlement_declined</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">failed</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">gateway_rejected</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">processor_declined</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">settled</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">settling</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">submitted_for_settlement</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">voided</span></li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><span class="langAttribute">timestamp</span></td><td><span>
                The date/time the status change was performed. Results are returned in
                UTC.
            </span></td></tr><tr><td><span class="langAttribute">transaction_source</span></td><td><span>
                How a transaction was created. Possible values:
                </span><ul class="list list--disc list list--disc"><li><span class="langAttribute">Api</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">ControlPanel</span></li><li><span class="langAttribute">Recurring</span></li></ul></td></tr><tr><td><span class="langAttribute">user</span></td><td><span>
                The Braintree Control Panel username of the person who performed an
                action that triggered the status change of the transaction.
            </span></td></tr></tbody></table><p class="markdown-p"><span>You can use these status events to retrieve information around transaction status changes.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><div class="styles_tab_container"><ol class="styles_tab_list"><div><li class="styles_tab_list_item styles_tab_list_active">Ruby</li></div></ol><div class="codeblock-spacing"><button class="copy-button" aria-label="Copy"><span class="copy-status">Copy</span><svg class="snippet__copy-icon" fill="#ffffff" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"></path><path d="M16 1H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14h2V3h12V1zm3 4H8c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h11c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V7c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 16H8V7h11v14z"></path></svg></button><pre class="language-ruby"><code class="language-ruby">transaction = gateway.transaction.find(&quot;the_transaction_id&quot;)
transaction.status_history.each do |event|
	puts event.amount
	puts event.status
	puts event.timestamp
	puts event.transaction_source
	puts event.user

end</code></pre></div></div></p><h2 id="product-id-codes" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Product ID codes</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#product-id-codes" aria-label="Product ID codes"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>The Braintree gateway returns the following product IDs for credit and debit card payment methods.

</div><h2 id="network-response-codes" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Network response codes</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#network-response-codes" aria-label="Network response codes"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>In addition to the </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#processor_response_code"><span>processor response code</span></a><span> and text, some transaction
    and verification objects also include a </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#network_response_code"><span>network response code</span></a><span> and text.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>These network response values are the raw responses that may be returned by the card network, and
    when present they can provide additional detail about why a request was approved or declined.
    However, this information is supplemental to the processor response code; you should consider the
    processor response code to be the source of truth.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Each card network has distinct response codes:</span></p><ul class="list list--disc"><li><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#card-network-visa"><span>Visa</span></a></li><li><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#card-network-mastercard"><span>Mastercard</span></a></li><li><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#card-network-discover"><span>Discover</span></a></li><li><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/#card-network-american-express"><span>American Express</span></a></li></ul><style data-emotion="css Transaction\nslug: /docs/reference/response/transaction/ruby/\ncreateTime: '2025-04-01T21:59:49.657Z'\nupdateTime: '2025-07-10T09:41:18.851Z'\n---\n\n\n\n# Transaction\n\n\n**NOTE**\nResults are limited according to the [PayPal Data Protection Addendum For Card Processing Products policy](https://www.paypal.com/us/legalhub/braintree/data-protection-addendum) .\n\nA record that includes all details of a transaction, including current [status](#status).\n\n\n## Result object\n\nRead more about [result objects](/braintree/docs/reference/general/result-objects/ruby).\n\n\n### Successful result\n\nIf the result is successful, the transaction will have either a[settling status](/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#settling),[authorized status](/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#authorized), or (if theoption was used) a[submitted for settlement status](/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#submitted-for-settlement).### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nresult.success?\n#=\u003e true\n\ntransaction = result.transaction\ntransaction.status\n#=\u003e \"authorized\"\n\n```\n\nAdditionally, you may inspect the result to determine if the transaction was created using a specific payment method type (e.g. PayPal account or a credit card), using the provided format.\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\ntransaction = result.transaction\ntransaction.payment_instrument_type == PaymentInstrumentType::PayPalAccount\n#=\u003e false\ntransaction.payment_instrument_type == PaymentInstrumentType::CreditCard\n#=\u003e true\n\n```\n\n\n### Unsuccessful result\n\nSuccess will return`{false}`if:\n- [Validations](#validation-errors)prevent the transaction from being created\n- The processor[declines the authorization](#processor-declined)or[settlement](#processor-settlement-declined)\n- The[gateway rejects](#gateway-rejection)the transaction\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nresult.success?\n#=\u003e false\n\nresult.errors\n\n```\n\n\n#### Validation errors\n\nIf any parameters are invalid, then the success call will return```syntax-inline\n`{false}`\n```\nand the[result object](/braintree/docs/reference/general/result-objects)will contain one or more[validation errors](/braintree/docs/reference/general/validation-errors/all)indicating which parameters were invalid.When receiving a validation error, a```syntax-inline\n\n```\nobject will not be present on the```syntax-inline\n\n```\nobject.\n#### Processor declined\n\nIf the processor [declines the transaction during the authorization](/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#processor-declined), the [processor response](/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses) will be available on the transaction object.\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nresult.success?\n#=\u003e false\nresult.transaction.status\n#=\u003e \"processor_declined\"\n\nresult.transaction.processor_response_type\n#=\u003e \"soft_declined\"\nresult.transaction.processor_response_code\n#=\u003e \"2001\"\nresult.transaction.processor_response_text\n#=\u003e \"Insufficient Funds\"\n\n```\n\nAs a supplement to the standardized processor response codes, we will return bank-specific Additional Processor Responses on the transaction object. The standardized code is what you should use when handling the result object, but the Additional Processor Response might provide further context.\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nresult.transaction.additional_processor_response\n# e.g. \"05 : NOT AUTHORISED\"\n\n```\n\n\n#### Processor settlement declined\n\nIf the processor [declines the transaction at the settlement stage](/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#settlement-declined), the [processor response](/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/settlement-responses) will be available on the transaction object.\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nresult.success?\n#=\u003e false\nresult.transaction.status\n#=\u003e \"settlement_declined\"\nresult.transaction.processor_settlement_response_code\n#=\u003e \"4001\"\nresult.transaction.processor_settlement_response_text\n#=\u003e \"Settlement Declined\"\n\n```\n\n\n#### Gateway rejection\n\nIf the transaction is [rejected by the gateway](/braintree/docs/reference/general/statuses#gateway-rejected) based on your account settings, you can check for the transaction status and gateway rejection reason.\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nresult.success?\n#=\u003e false\nresult.transaction.status\n#=\u003e \"gateway_rejected\"\nresult.transaction.gateway_rejection_reason\n#=\u003e e.g. \"cvv\"\n\n```\n\n\n#### Risk data\n\nWe return the risk data on credit card verifications and on transactions with [all compatible payment methods](/braintree/docs/guides/premium-fraud-management-tools/overview#compatibility). The data includes the fraud service provider, the risk identifier, the device data captured flag, and the risk decision, which can provide further context on how a verification or transaction was scored by our Premium Fraud Management Tools. For users of Fraud Protection, the data will include the decision reasons. For users of Fraud Protection Advanced, the data will also include the risk score.\n\n**NOTE**\n\n{' '} For users of our Java and.NET SDKs, you will need to upgrade to versions.NET 5.4.0 and Java 3.7.0 or later to see the decision reasons and risk score in the risk data.{' '}\n\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nresult.transaction.risk_data.id\n#=\u003e \"1SG23YHM4BT5\"\nresult.transaction.risk_data.decision\n#=\u003e \"Decline\"\nresult.transaction.risk_data.device_data_captured\n#=\u003e true\nresult.transaction.risk_data.fraud_service_provider\n#=\u003e \"Kount\"\nresult.transaction.risk_data.decision_reasons\n#=\u003e [\"reason1\", \"reason2\"]\nresult.transaction.risk_data.risk_score\n#=\u003e 42\n\n```\n\n\nThe possible values of the risk decision are:\n\n\n- \"Not Evaluated\"\n- \"Approve\"\n- \"Review\"\n- \"Decline\"\n\n\n#### Params retrieval\n\nSee our documentation on [result objects](/braintree/docs/reference/general/result-objects/ruby#params).\n\n\n## Examples\n\n\n### Currencies\n\nEach merchant account can only process transactions for a single currency. [Setting which merchant account to use](/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/sale/ruby#specify-merchant-account-id) will also determine which currency the transaction is processed with.\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nresult.transaction.currency_iso_code\n#=\u003e \"USD\"\n\n```\n\n\n### Settlement status\n\nCheck the result for success, and if it has failed, then first check for validation errors. If there are no validation errors, inspect the```syntax-inline\n`processor_settlement_response_code`\n```\non the transaction, which will indicate if the processor declined the request.### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nif result.success?\n  # transaction successfully submitted for settlement\nelsif result.errors.any?\n  puts result.errors.inspect\nelse\n  puts result.transaction.processor_settlement_response_code\n  puts result.transaction.processor_settlement_response_text\nend\n\n```\n\n\n#### Processor settlement declined\n\nIf the settlement request is declined by the processor, the [processor response](/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/settlement-responses) will be available on the transaction object.\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\nresult.success?\n#=\u003e false\nresult.transaction.status\n#=\u003e \"settlement_declined\"\nresult.transaction.processor_settlement_response_code\n#=\u003e \"4001\"\nresult.transaction.processor_settlement_response_text\n#=\u003e \"Settlement Declined\"\n\n```\n\n\n### Voiding settlement\n\nIf you submit a transaction for settlement and then decide you actually don't want to settle it, you can [void](/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/void) it before it's settled. After it's settled, you'll need to [refund](/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/refund) it instead.\n\nTo check if the transaction has been settled, find the transaction and check the status.\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\n    transaction = gateway.transaction.find(\"the_transaction_id\")\n    if transaction.status == \"submitted_for_settlement\"\n      # can void\n    elsif transaction.status == \"settled\"\n      # will have to refund it\n    else\n      # this example only expected one of the two above statuses\n    end\n\n```\n\n\n## Authorization adjustments\n\nThe authorized amount of a transaction can be adjusted by using the [adjust authorization](/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/adjust-authorization) endpoint. This will cause an authorization adjustment to be performed.\n\nWhen submitting a transaction for settlement, if you [specify a settlement amount that is different than the authorized amount](/braintree/docs/reference/request/transaction/submit-for-settlement/ruby#specifying-settlement-amount), an authorization adjustment may be performed automatically.\n\nFor each adjustment performed, an authorization adjustment object will be associated with the original transaction. These adjustment objects will include the following details:\n\n| Adjustment Detail | Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| `amount` | The difference between the authorized amount and the amount submitted for settlement. Negative values indicate the authorized amount was adjusted down. |\n| `success` | A boolean value indicating if the adjustment was successful. |\n| `timestamp` | The date/time when the adjustment was performed. |\n| `proccessor_response_type` | The processor response type. Possible values:{' '}```syntax-inline\n\"approved\"\n```\n,{' '}```syntax-inline\n\"soft_declined\"\n```\n,{' '}```syntax-inline\n\"hard_declined\"\n```\n. See the list of{' '}[possible processor authorization responses.](/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses) |\n| `proccessor_response_code` | The processor response code. See the list of{' '}[possible processor authorization responses.](/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses) |\n| `proccessor_response_text` | The processor response text. See the list of{' '}[possible processor authorization responses.](/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses) |\n\n\n## Status history details\n\n\n\n| Status Detail | Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| `amount` | The amount of the request. |\n| `status` | A record of the statuses that a transaction has progressed through. Possible values:\n- `authorization_expired`\n- `authorized`\n- `authorizing`\n- `settlement_pending`\n- `settlement_confirmed`\n- `settlement_declined`\n- `failed`\n- `gateway_rejected`\n- `processor_declined`\n- `settled`\n- `settling`\n- `submitted_for_settlement`\n- `voided` |\n| `timestamp` | The date/time the status change was performed. Results are returned in UTC. |\n| `transaction_source` | How a transaction was created. Possible values:\n- `Api`\n- `ControlPanel`\n- `Recurring` |\n| `user` | The Braintree Control Panel username of the person who performed an action that triggered the status change of the transaction. |\n\nYou can use these status events to retrieve information around transaction status changes.\n\n### Ruby\n```ruby\n\ntransaction = gateway.transaction.find(\"the_transaction_id\")\ntransaction.status_history.each do |event|\n\tputs event.amount\n\tputs event.status\n\tputs event.timestamp\n\tputs event.transaction_source\n\tputs event.user\n\nend\n\n```\n\n\n## Product ID codes\n\nThe Braintree gateway returns the following product IDs for credit and debit card payment methods. The product ID is generally 1-3 characters and indicates the specific credit product that was issued to the customer.\n\n\n\n## Network response codes\n\nIn addition to the [processor response code](#processor_response_code) and text, some transaction and verification objects also include a [network response code](#network_response_code) and text.\n\nThese network response values are the raw responses that may be returned by the card network, and when present they can provide additional detail about why a request was approved or declined. However, this information is supplemental to the processor response code; you should consider the processor response code to be the source of truth.\n\nEach card network has distinct response codes:\n\n\n- [Visa](#card-network-visa)\n- [Mastercard](#card-network-mastercard)\n- [Discover](#card-network-discover)\n- [American Express](#card-network-american-express)\n\n| Card Network | Code | Text |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| Visa | 00 | Successful approval/completion or V.I.P. PIN verification is successful |\n| Visa | 01 | Refer to card issuer |\n| Visa | 02 | Refer to card issuer, special condition |\n| Visa | 03 | Invalid merchant or service provider |\n| Visa | 04 | Pick up card |\n| Visa | 05 | Do not Honor |\n| Visa | 06 | Error |\n| Visa | 07 | Pick up card, special condition (other than lost/stolen card) |\n| Visa | 10 | Partial Approval |\n| Visa | 11 | V.I.P. approval |\n| Visa | 12 | Invalid transaction |\n| Visa | 13 | Invalid amount (currency conversion field overflow); or amount exceeds maximum for card program |\n| Visa | 14 | Invalid account number (no such number) |\n| Visa | 15 | No such issuer |\n| Visa | 19 | Re-enter transaction |\n| Visa | 21 | No action taken (unable to back out prior transaction) |\n| Visa | 25 | Unable to locate record in file, or account number is missing from the inquiry |\n| Visa | 28 | File is temporarily unavailable |\n| Visa | 39 | No credit account |\n| Visa | 41 | Pick up card (lost card) |\n| Visa | 43 | Pick up card (stolen card) |\n| Visa | 46 | Closed Account |\n| Visa | 51 | Insufficient funds |\n| Visa | 52 | No checking account |\n| Visa | 53 | No savings account |\n| Visa | 54 | Expired card |\n| Visa | 55 | Incorrect PIN |\n| Visa | 57 | Transaction not permitted to cardholder |\n| Visa | 58 | Transaction not allowed at terminal |\n| Visa | 59 | Suspected fraud |\n| Visa | 61 | Activity amount limit exceeded |\n| Visa | 62 | Restricted card (for instance, in Country Exclusion table) |\n| Visa | 63 | Security violation |\n| Visa | 64 | Transaction does not fulfill AML requirement |\n| Visa | 65 | Activity count limit exceeded |\n| Visa | 75 | Allowable number of PIN-entry tries exceeded |\n| Visa | 76 | Unable to locate previous message (no match on retrieval reference number) |\n| Visa | 77 | Previous message located for a repeat or reversal, but repeat or reversal data inconsistent with original message |\n| Visa | 78 | Blocked, first used  Transaction from new cardholder, and card not properly unblocked |\n| Visa | 79 | Transaction reversed |\n| Visa | 80 | Visa transactions: credit issuer unavailable. Private label: invalid date |\n| Visa | 81 | PIN cryptographic error found (error found by VIC security module during PIN decryption) |\n| Visa | 82 | Negative Online CAM, dCVV, iCVV, or CVV results Or Offline PIN authentication interrupted |\n| Visa | 85 | No reason to decline request for account number verification, address verification, CVV2 verification, or credit voucher or merchandise return |\n| Visa | 86 | Cannot verify PIN |\n| Visa | 91 | Issuer unavailable or switch inoperative (STIP not applicable or available for this transaction) Issuers can respond with this code, which V.I.P. passes to the acquirer without invoking stand-in processing (STIP).
